### 帖子 #27: regular + asiregular + asi  +DELAY 1#暂时未考虑翻页region_now = "EUR"if region_now == "ASI":    results = wait_get(s,"https://api.worldquantbrain.com/users/self/alphas?limit=100&offset=0&status!=UNSUBMITTED%1FIS-FAIL&type=REGULAR&settings.region=ASI&order=-dateCreated&hidden=false").json()elif region_now == "USA":    results = wait_get(s,"https://api.worldquantbrain.com/users/self/alphas?limit=100&offset=0&status!=UNSUBMITTED%1FIS-FAIL&settings.region=USA&settings.delay=1&type=REGULAR&order=-settings.region&hidden=false").json()elif region_now == "GLB":    results = wait_get(s,"https://api.worldquantbrain.com/users/self/alphas?limit=100&offset=0&status!=UNSUBMITTED%1FIS-FAIL&settings.region=GLB&settings.delay=1&type=REGULAR&order=-settings.region&hidden=false").json()elif region_now == "EUR":    results = wait_get(s,"https://api.worldquantbrain.com/users/self/alphas?limit=100&offset=0&status!=UNSUBMITTED%1FIS-FAIL&settings.region=EUR&settings.delay=1&type=REGULAR&order=-settings.region&hidden=false").json()
- **主帖链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com【代码优化】三步构建PPA的Alpha组合从筛选评分到分类选拔_33708756373015.md
- **讨论数**: 0

**问题背景** ：因为Combined Power Pool Alpha Performance的出现，给了大家一个可以自己构建ppa组合的机会。因为我的combine实在是不高，想着可以通过构建高质量的ppa的组合来获取一个过得去的combine。（前提是：增删tag确实可以改变参与计算Combined Power Pool Alpha Performance的alpha，希望本文有点帮助吧）

**处理流程描述** ：先选出所有的ppa，然后进行下列的筛选。

1.硬性质量筛选：确保所有候选者都满足最基本的生存标准。我提供了一些初步的筛选标准，这里是可以自由发挥的，仁者见仁智者见智。我的条件如下：

fitness>0.8,margin>0.0015,至少有8年数据，至少6年sharpe大于1，负sharpe年份最多两年，2020-2022三年平均sharpe大于1，平均returns/turnover > 0.75，return>drawdown的年份至少7年。

2.综合评分排序：筛选出满足第1点的ppa之后，然后进行打分。这里用4个指标进行打分：

'fitness': 'higher_is_better',

'returns_over_turnover': 'higher_is_better',

'margin': 'higher_is_better',

'return_to_drawdown': 'higher_is_better'

就是fitness，return和turnover的比值，margin，return和drawdown的比值。这里也是可以自由发挥，仁者见仁智者见智。然后四个指标转换为0-100分，然后自己可以赋个权重。最后得到一个总分。

3.分类选秀构建：通过组合构建算法，实现质量和多样性的统一。

接着的话就是选取alpha进行构建了。然后的话，一般池子里的alpha的相关性要低一点，我希望池子里的alpha两两的相关性小于0.35，这里也可以调成自己喜欢的值。

筛选的逻辑是：先按照neutralization进行分组，每组的按照分数从大到小排序。把分数排名第一的alpha的组排第一个，其余的组随意排。然后从第一个组的第一个alpha开始，这个alpha分数最高，目前池子里一个alpha没有，直接进入池子。然后遍历第二个组的alpha，计算每个alpha与池子里alpha（当前只有一个）的相关性，选取第一个小于0.35的alpha进入池子，即第二个组选择第一个相关性小于0.35的alpha，然后退出第二个组遍历，如果这个组里的alpha全部大于0.35，那就一个不选。接着遍历第三个组的。然后第一组遍历完后，开始第二轮遍历。直到所有的alpha都遍历一遍，最终得到一个alpha的组合。

**代码实现** ：

预先准备：

```
# 导入官方库import jsonimport osimport requestsfrom requests.auth import HTTPBasicAuthimport timeimport winsound# 导入第三方库from dotenv import load_dotenv  # 导入环境变量，非必需 pip install python-dotenvimport matplotlib.pyplot as pltimport pandas as pdfrom collections import defaultdictfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutorimport loggingimport osfrom pathlib import Pathimport pickleimport requestsimport timefrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple# 导入第三方库from dotenv import load_dotenv  # 导入环境变量，非必需 pip install python-dotenvimport pandas as pdimport numpy as npimport pandas as pdfrom IPython.display import display  # 导入 display 函数# 读取环境变量文件load_dotenv()class cfg:    data_path = Path('./data')def save_obj(obj: object, name: str) -> None:    """    保存对象到文件中，以 pickle 格式序列化。    Args:        obj (object): 需要保存的对象。        name (str): 文件名（不包含扩展名），保存的文件将以 '.pickle' 为扩展名。    Returns:        None: 此函数无返回值。    Raises:        pickle.PickleError: 如果序列化过程中发生错误。        IOError: 如果文件写入过程中发生 I/O 错误。    """    with open(name + '.pickle', 'wb') as f:        pickle.dump(obj, f, pickle.HIGHEST_PROTOCOL)def load_obj(name: str) -> object:    """    加载指定名称的 pickle 文件并返回其内容。    此函数会打开一个以 `.pickle` 为扩展名的文件，并使用 `pickle` 模块加载其内容。    Args:        name (str): 不带扩展名的文件名称。    Returns:        object: 从 pickle 文件中加载的 Python 对象。    Raises:        FileNotFoundError: 如果指定的文件不存在。        pickle.UnpicklingError: 如果文件内容无法被正确反序列化。    """    with open(name + '.pickle', 'rb') as f:        return pickle.load(f)def wait_get(s,url: str, max_retries: int = 10) -> "Response":    """    发送带有重试机制的 GET 请求，直到成功或达到最大重试次数。    此函数会根据服务器返回的 `Retry-After` 头信息进行等待，并在遇到 401 状态码时重新初始化配置。    Args:        url (str): 目标 URL。        max_retries (int, optional): 最大重试次数，默认为 10。    Returns:        Response: 请求的响应对象。    """    retries = 0    while retries < max_retries:        while True:            simulation_progress = s.get(url)            if simulation_progress.headers.get("Retry-After", 0) == 0:                break            time.sleep(float(simulation_progress.headers["Retry-After"]))        if simulation_progress.status_code < 400:            break        else:            time.sleep(2 ** retries)            retries += 1    return simulation_progress#---------------------------def _get_alpha_pnl(s,alpha_id: str) -> pd.DataFrame:    """    获取指定 alpha 的 PnL数据，并返回一个包含日期和 PnL 的 DataFrame。    此函数通过调用 WorldQuant Brain API 获取指定 alpha 的 PnL 数据，    并将其转换为 pandas DataFrame 格式，方便后续数据处理。    Args:        alpha_id (str): Alpha 的唯一标识符。    Returns:        pd.DataFrame: 包含日期和对应 PnL 数据的 DataFrame，列名为 'Date' 和 alpha_id。    """    pnl = wait_get(s,"[链接已屏蔽] + alpha_id + "/recordsets/pnl").json()    df = pd.DataFrame(pnl['records'], columns=[item['name'] for item in pnl['schema']['properties']])    df = df.rename(columns={'date':'Date', 'pnl':alpha_id})    df = df[['Date', alpha_id]]    return dfdef get_alpha_pnls(s,    alphas: list[dict],    alpha_pnls: Optional[pd.DataFrame] = None,    alpha_ids: Optional[dict[str, list]] = None) -> Tuple[dict[str, list], pd.DataFrame]:    """    获取 alpha 的 PnL 数据，并按区域分类 alpha 的 ID。    Args:        alphas (list[dict]): 包含 alpha 信息的列表，每个元素是一个字典，包含 alpha 的 ID 和设置等信息。        alpha_pnls (Optional[pd.DataFrame], 可选): 已有的 alpha PnL 数据，默认为空的 DataFrame。        alpha_ids (Optional[dict[str, list]], 可选): 按区域分类的 alpha ID 字典，默认为空字典。    Returns:        Tuple[dict[str, list], pd.DataFrame]:            - 按区域分类的 alpha ID 字典。            - 包含所有 alpha 的 PnL 数据的 DataFrame。    """    # 如果alpha_ids字典没有传入，则生成一个默认值为list()的字典存储alpha_id以及一个dataframe存储alpha_pnls    if alpha_ids is None:        alpha_ids = defaultdict(list)    if alpha_pnls is None:        alpha_pnls = pd.DataFrame()    # 筛选新增的alpha_id    new_alphas = [item for item in alphas if item['id'] not in alpha_pnls.columns]    if not new_alphas:        return alpha_ids, alpha_pnls    # 在alpha_ids字典中的对应region增加新增的alpha_id    print(666)    for item_alpha in new_alphas:        alpha_ids[item_alpha['settings']['region']].append(item_alpha['id'])    # 使用线程池并发对多个alpha_ids批量抓取PnL数据    fetch_pnl_func = lambda alpha_id: _get_alpha_pnl(s,alpha_id).set_index('Date')    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=10) as executor:        results = executor.map(fetch_pnl_func, [item['id'] for item in new_alphas])    # 把获取的alpha_pnls和已有的PnL数据合并为一个dataframe，并按日期升序排列    alpha_pnls = pd.concat([alpha_pnls] + list(results), axis=1)    alpha_pnls.sort_index(inplace=True)    return alpha_ids, alpha_pnlsdef get_os_alphas(s,limit: int = 100, get_first: bool = False) -> List[Dict]:    """    获取OS阶段的alpha列表。    此函数通过调用WorldQuant Brain API获取用户的alpha列表，支持分页获取，并可以选择只获取第一个结果。    Args:        limit (int, optional): 每次请求获取的alpha数量限制。默认为100。        get_first (bool, optional): 是否只获取第一次请求的alpha结果。如果为True，则只请求一次。默认为False。    Returns:        List[Dict]: 包含alpha信息的字典列表，每个字典表示一个alpha。    """    fetched_alphas = []    offset = 0    retries = 0    total_alphas = 100    while len(fetched_alphas) < total_alphas:        print(f"Fetching alphas from offset {offset} to {offset + limit}")        url = f"[链接已屏蔽]        res = wait_get(s,url).json()        if offset == 0:            total_alphas = res['count']        alphas = res["results"]        fetched_alphas.extend(alphas)        if len(alphas) < limit:            break        offset += limit        if get_first:            break    return fetched_alphas[:total_alphas]def download_data(s,flag_increment=True):    """    下载数据并保存到指定路径。    此函数会检查数据是否已经存在，如果不存在，则从 API 下载数据并保存到指定路径。    Args:        flag_increment (bool): 是否使用增量下载，默认为 True。    """    # 根据是否增量下载给变量赋值    if flag_increment:        try:            os_alpha_ids = load_obj(str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_ids'))            os_alpha_pnls = load_obj(str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_pnls'))            ppac_alpha_ids = load_obj(str(cfg.data_path / 'ppac_alpha_ids'))            exist_alpha = [alpha for ids in os_alpha_ids.values() for alpha in ids]        except Exception as e:            logging.error(f"Failed to load existing data: {e}")            os_alpha_ids = None            os_alpha_pnls = None            exist_alpha = []            ppac_alpha_ids = []    else:        os_alpha_ids = None        os_alpha_pnls = None        exist_alpha = []        ppac_alpha_ids = []    # 增量/全量获取已提交alpha信息    if os_alpha_ids is None:        alphas = get_os_alphas(s,limit=100, get_first=False)    else:        alphas = get_os_alphas(s,limit=30, get_first=True)  # 可以根据实际情况调整limit    # 筛选新增alpha_id的数据    alphas = [item for item in alphas if item['id'] not in exist_alpha]    # 获取符合ppac theme的alpha_ids    ppac_alpha_ids += [item['id'] for item in alphas for item_match in item['classifications'] if item_match['name'] == 'Power Pool Alpha']    # 获取全量的alpha_pnls以及全量alpha_ids和ppac主题alpha_ids，并保存为pickle文件    os_alpha_ids, os_alpha_pnls = get_alpha_pnls(s,alphas, alpha_pnls=os_alpha_pnls, alpha_ids=os_alpha_ids)    save_obj(os_alpha_ids, str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_ids'))    save_obj(os_alpha_pnls, str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_pnls'))    save_obj(ppac_alpha_ids, str(cfg.data_path / 'ppac_alpha_ids'))    print(f'新下载的alpha数量: {len(alphas)}, 目前总共alpha数量: {os_alpha_pnls.shape[1]}')def load_data(tag=None):    """    加载数据。    此函数会检查数据是否已经存在，如果不存在，则从 API 下载数据并保存到指定路径。    Args:        tag (str): 数据标记，默认为 None。    """    # 读取pickle文件    os_alpha_ids = load_obj(str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_ids'))    os_alpha_pnls = load_obj(str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_pnls'))    ppac_alpha_ids = load_obj(str(cfg.data_path / 'ppac_alpha_ids'))    # 根据tag筛选alpha_pnls    if tag=='PPAC':        for item in os_alpha_ids:            os_alpha_ids[item] = [alpha for alpha in os_alpha_ids[item] if alpha in ppac_alpha_ids]    elif tag=='SelfCorr':        for item in os_alpha_ids:            os_alpha_ids[item] = [alpha for alpha in os_alpha_ids[item] if alpha not in ppac_alpha_ids]    else:        os_alpha_ids = os_alpha_ids    exist_alpha = [alpha for ids in os_alpha_ids.values() for alpha in ids]    os_alpha_pnls = os_alpha_pnls[exist_alpha]    # 计算已提交alpha的日度收益率并截取近4年数据    os_alpha_rets = os_alpha_pnls - os_alpha_pnls.ffill().shift(1)    os_alpha_rets = os_alpha_rets[pd.to_datetime(os_alpha_rets.index)>pd.to_datetime(os_alpha_rets.index).max() - pd.DateOffset(years=4)]    return os_alpha_ids, os_alpha_rets#------------------def calc_self_corr(s,    alpha_id: str,    os_alpha_rets: pd.DataFrame | None = None,    os_alpha_ids: dict[str, str] | None = None,    alpha_result: dict | None = None,    return_alpha_pnls: bool = False,    alpha_pnls: pd.DataFrame | None = None) -> float | tuple[float, pd.DataFrame]:    """    计算指定 alpha 与其他 alpha 的最大自相关性。    Args:        alpha_id (str): 目标 alpha 的唯一标识符。        os_alpha_rets (pd.DataFrame | None, optional): 其他 alpha 的收益率数据，默认为 None。        os_alpha_ids (dict[str, str] | None, optional): 其他 alpha 的标识符映射，默认为 None。        alpha_result (dict | None, optional): 目标 alpha 的详细信息，默认为 None。        return_alpha_pnls (bool, optional): 是否返回 alpha 的 PnL 数据，默认为 False。        alpha_pnls (pd.DataFrame | None, optional): 目标 alpha 的 PnL 数据，默认为 None。    Returns:        float | tuple[float, pd.DataFrame]: 如果 `return_alpha_pnls` 为 False，返回最大自相关性值；            如果 `return_alpha_pnls` 为 True，返回包含最大自相关性值和 alpha PnL 数据的元组。    """    # 按需获取alpha_result    if alpha_result is None:        alpha_result = wait_get(s,f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()       # 按需获取alpha_pnls    if alpha_pnls is not None:        if len(alpha_pnls) == 0:            alpha_pnls = None    if alpha_pnls is None:        _, alpha_pnls = get_alpha_pnls(s,[alpha_result])        alpha_pnls = alpha_pnls[alpha_id]    # 计算因子的日度收益率    alpha_rets = alpha_pnls - alpha_pnls.ffill().shift(1)    # 截取最近4年数据    alpha_rets = alpha_rets[pd.to_datetime(alpha_rets.index)>pd.to_datetime(alpha_rets.index).max() - pd.DateOffset(years=4)]    # 打印结果到控制台    print(os_alpha_rets[os_alpha_ids[alpha_result['settings']['region']]].corrwith(alpha_rets).sort_values(ascending=False).round(4))    # 按需决定是否需要保存到csv文件    # os_alpha_rets[os_alpha_ids[alpha_result['settings']['region']]].corrwith(alpha_rets).sort_values(ascending=False).round(4).to_csv(str(cfg.data_path / 'os_alpha_corr.csv'))    # 返回最大值    self_corr = os_alpha_rets[os_alpha_ids[alpha_result['settings']['region']]].corrwith(alpha_rets).abs().max()    if np.isnan(self_corr):        self_corr = 0    if return_alpha_pnls:        return self_corr, alpha_pnls    else:        return self_corr   def login():    """    Log in to the WorldQuant API using credentials stored in environment variables.    This function creates a session that includes authentication credentials from environment    variables and sends a POST request to the WorldQuant API's authentication endpoint. The    response content is printed, and the session is returned for further interaction with the    API.    Returns:        requests.Session: A session object with authentication credentials and headers.    Raises:        Any exceptions raised by the `requests` library during the network operations are        propagated to the caller.    """    username = ""    password = ""    # Create a session to persistently store the headers    s = requests.Session()    # Save credentials into session    s.auth = (username, password)    # Send a POST request to the /authentication API    response = s.post('[链接已屏蔽])    print(response.content)    return sdef locate_alpha(s, alpha_id):    """    Retrieve and parse alpha data from an API.    This function sends an HTTP GET request to retrieve alpha data from a specified    API using the given alpha identifier. Upon receiving a response, it checks for    rate-limiting headers and waits if necessary. The function then decodes the    response content, extracts relevant performance metrics and alpha settings,    and returns them in a list.    Parameters:        s (Session): A requests.Session object used for making the HTTP GET request.        alpha_id (str): The unique identifier for the alpha to be retrieved.    Returns:        list: A list containing extracted alpha data, including            - alpha_id (str)            - sharpe (float)            - turnover (float)            - fitness (float)            - margin (float)            - expr (str): Alpha's code expression.            - region (str): Associated region of the alpha.            - universe (str): Universe setting for the alpha.            - neutralization (str): Neutralization setting.            - decay (float)            - truncation (float)    """    while True:        alpha = s.get("[链接已屏蔽] + alpha_id)        if "retry-after" in alpha.headers:            time.sleep(float(alpha.headers["Retry-After"]))        else:            break    string = alpha.content.decode('utf-8')    metrics = json.loads(string)    sharpe = metrics["is"]["sharpe"]    fitness = metrics["is"]["fitness"]    turnover = metrics["is"]["turnover"]    margin = metrics["is"]["margin"]    decay = metrics["settings"]["decay"]    delay = metrics["settings"]["delay"]    exp = metrics['regular']['code']    universe=metrics["settings"]["universe"]    truncation=metrics["settings"]["truncation"]    neutralization=metrics["settings"]["neutralization"]    region=metrics["settings"]["region"]    returns = metrics["is"]["returns"]    triple = [alpha_id, sharpe, turnover, fitness, margin, exp, region, universe, neutralization, decay, delay, truncation,returns]    return tripledef get_pnl(s, alpha_id):    """    Fetches the profit and loss (PnL) data for a given alpha ID by making requests to an API endpoint.    The function handles retry logic for requests when a 'Retry-After' header    is present in the response from the server.    Parameters:        s: requests.Session            The session object used to make requests to the API.        alpha_id: str            The unique identifier of the alpha whose PnL data is to be fetched.    Returns:        requests.Response            The API response containing PnL data.    Raises:        No explicit exceptions are raised within the function, but exceptions        related to HTTP requests (such as connection errors) may occur.    """    while True:        pnl = s.get('[链接已屏蔽] + alpha_id + '/recordsets/pnl')        if pnl.headers.get('Retry-After', 0) == 0:             break        time.sleep(float(pnl.headers['Retry-After']))    return pnldef get_power_pool_alphas(alpha_list):    """    从alpha列表中提取所有包含POWER_POOL:POWER_POOL_ELIGIBLE分类的alpha ID       参数:        alpha_list: 包含多个alpha字典的列表           返回:        包含符合条件的alpha ID的列表    """    power_pool_alphas = []       for alpha in alpha_list:        # 检查是否存在classifications字段        if "classifications" in alpha:            # 遍历classifications中的每一项            for classification in alpha["classifications"]:                # 检查是否有POWER_POOL:POWER_POOL_ELIGIBLE                if classification.get("id") == "POWER_POOL:POWER_POOL_ELIGIBLE":                    power_pool_alphas.append(alpha["id"])                    break  # 找到后就跳出循环，继续下一个alpha       return power_pool_alphasdef wait_get(s,url: str, max_retries: int = 10) -> "Response":    """    发送带有重试机制的 GET 请求，直到成功或达到最大重试次数。    此函数会根据服务器返回的 `Retry-After` 头信息进行等待，并在遇到 401 状态码时重新初始化配置。    Args:        url (str): 目标 URL。        max_retries (int, optional): 最大重试次数，默认为 10。    Returns:        Response: 请求的响应对象。    """    retries = 0    while retries < max_retries:        while True:            simulation_progress = s.get(url)            if simulation_progress.headers.get("Retry-After", 0) == 0:                break            time.sleep(float(simulation_progress.headers["Retry-After"]))        if simulation_progress.status_code < 400:            break        else:            time.sleep(2 ** retries)            retries += 1    return simulation_progressdef check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):    # Get the yearly stats data    a = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()    b = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()    sharpe = b['is']['sharpe']    fitness = b['is']['fitness']    returns = b['is']['returns']    drawdown = b['is']['drawdown']    turnover = b['is']['turnover']    margin = b['is']['margin']    stage1 = fitness > 0.8 and margin > 0.0015  and drawdown < 0.25       data = a['records']       # Extract sharpe values (7th parameter in each record, index 6)    sharpe_values = [float(record[6]) for record in data]       # Check conditions:    # 1. At least 8 years with sharpe != 0    non_zero_sharpe = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe != 0)    condition1 = non_zero_sharpe >= 8       # 2. At least 6 years with sharpe > 1    sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe > 1)    condition2 = sharpe_above_1 >= 6    # sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe > 0)    # condition3 = sharpe_above_1 >= 11  #所有年份sharpe为正    sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe < 0)    condition3 = sharpe_above_1 <= 2  #负年份只允许有2年    condition4 = (data[7][6]+data[8][6]+data[9][6])/3 > 1   #最近三年shapre平均值大于1    stage2 = condition1 and  condition2 and condition3 and condition4    stage3 = returns/turnover > 0.75  and  not any(record[8] >= 0.15 for record in data)    print(alpha_id+":sharpe检测:"+str(stage1 and stage2  and stage3))    print("stage1:"+str(stage1)+"stage2:"+str(stage2)+"stage3:"+str(stage3))       # Return True if both conditions are met    return stage1 and stage2  and stage3  #2022年的sharpe大于1def set_alpha_properties(        s,        alpha_id,        name: str = None,        color: str = None,        selection_desc: str = None,        combo_desc: str = None,        tags: list = None,  # ['tag1', 'tag2']):    """    Function changes alpha's description parameters    """    params = {        "category": None,        "regular": {"description": None},    }    if color:        params["color"] = color    if name:        params["name"] = name    if tags:        params["tags"] = tags    if combo_desc:        params["combo"] = {"description": combo_desc}    if selection_desc:        params["selection"] = {"description": selection_desc}    response = s.patch(        "[链接已屏蔽] + alpha_id, json=params    )#下面为计算相关性的函数def _get_alpha_pnl(s,alpha_id: str) -> pd.DataFrame:    """    获取指定 alpha 的 PnL数据，并返回一个包含日期和 PnL 的 DataFrame。    此函数通过调用 WorldQuant Brain API 获取指定 alpha 的 PnL 数据，    并将其转换为 pandas DataFrame 格式，方便后续数据处理。    Args:        alpha_id (str): Alpha 的唯一标识符。    Returns:        pd.DataFrame: 包含日期和对应 PnL 数据的 DataFrame，列名为 'Date' 和 alpha_id。    """    pnl = wait_get(s,"[链接已屏蔽] + alpha_id + "/recordsets/pnl").json()    df = pd.DataFrame(pnl['records'], columns=[item['name'] for item in pnl['schema']['properties']])    df = df.rename(columns={'date':'Date', 'pnl':alpha_id})    df = df[['Date', alpha_id]]    return df
```

然后正式开始（需要你在login函数里面填一下你的信息）：

```
s = login()
```

```
# regular + asi# regular + asi  +DELAY 1#暂时未考虑翻页region_now = "EUR"if region_now == "ASI":    results = wait_get(s,"[链接已屏蔽]).json()elif region_now == "USA":    results = wait_get(s,"[链接已屏蔽]).json()elif region_now == "GLB":    results = wait_get(s,"[链接已屏蔽]).json()elif region_now == "EUR":    results = wait_get(s,"[链接已屏蔽]).json()
```

上面的变量中region_now 选择你需要构建ppa的地区，下面的api对应的意思是，在submit界面中，依次选择条件region，regular，delay。因为我只做delay1的，delay我就不选择了。然后region的话是四个地区，你可以改改。然后我只选择了第一页的alpha，因为我每个地区提交的alpha都没有超过100个，所以不需要第二页，如果你超过了还要加一点offset的分页的代码。

```
ppac_id_list = get_power_pool_alphas(results["results"])
```

然后选出所有的ppa的alpha，逻辑是ppa的alpha都有一个POWER_POOL:POWER_POOL_ELIGIBLE，检查这个有没有就可以了。

然后是第一轮的筛选，所有条件写成的函数如下：

```
def check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):    # Get the yearly stats data    a = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()    b = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()    sharpe = b['is']['sharpe']    fitness = b['is']['fitness']    returns = b['is']['returns']    drawdown = b['is']['drawdown']    turnover = b['is']['turnover']    margin = b['is']['margin']    # return_to_drawdown_ratio = returns / drawdown if drawdown > 0 else float('inf')    stage1=fitness>0.8andmargin>0.0015       data = a['records']       # Extract sharpe values (7th parameter in each record, index 6)    sharpe_values = [float(record[6]) for record in data]       # Check conditions:    # 1. At least 8 years with sharpe != 0    non_zero_sharpe = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe != 0)    condition1 = non_zero_sharpe >= 8       # 2. At least 6 years with sharpe > 1    sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe > 1)    condition2 = sharpe_above_1 >= 6    # sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe > 0)    # condition3 = sharpe_above_1 >= 11  #所有年份sharpe为正    sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe < 0)    condition3 = sharpe_above_1 <= 2  #负年份只允许有2年    condition4 = (data[7][6]+data[8][6]+data[9][6])/3 > 1   #最近三年shapre平均值大于1    stage2 = condition1 and  condition2 and condition3 and condition4       good_years_count = sum(1 for rec in data if rec[5] > 0 and ((rec[8] > 0 and rec[7] / rec[8] > 1) or (rec[8] == 0 and rec[7] > 0)))  #希望returns和drawdown的比值大于1的年份至少7年    yearly_performance_condition = good_years_count >= 7 # 假设阈值是7年    # not any(record[8] >= 0.15 for record in data)    stage3 = returns/turnover > 0.75  and   yearly_performance_condition    print(alpha_id+":sharpe检测:"+str(stage1 and stage2  and stage3))    print("stage1:"+str(stage1)+"stage2:"+str(stage2)+"stage3:"+str(stage3))       # Return True if both conditions are met    return stage1 and stage2  and stage3
```

然后检查所有的ppa中满足上面条件的alpha：

```
filtered_ids = []for alpha_id in ppac_id_list:    if check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):  # 假设 s 是已经定义的 session 对象        filtered_ids.append(alpha_id)
```

然后是第二点的打分，为了打分，先获取通过筛选的ppa的一些信息：

```
metrics_list = []   for alpha_id in filtered_ids:    try:        # 获取 alpha 数据        a = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()               # 提取 is 字典中的关键指标        is_data = a.get("is", {})        metrics = {            "id": alpha_id,            "sharpe": is_data.get("sharpe"),            "fitness": is_data.get("fitness"),            "turnover": is_data.get("turnover"),            "returns": is_data.get("returns"),            "drawdown": is_data.get("drawdown"),            "margin": is_data.get("margin"),            "neutralization" : a["settings"]["neutralization"]        }        metrics_list.append(metrics)           except Exception as e:        print(f"Error processing alpha {alpha_id}: {e}")        continue# 转换为 DataFramedf = pd.DataFrame(metrics_list)# 设置列顺序（id 第一列）# column_order = ["id", "sharpe", "fitness", "turnover", "returns", "drawdown", "margin","neutralization"]# df = df[column_order]
```

然后写出具体的打分的函数：

```
def calculate_comprehensive_score(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:    """    为DataFrame中的每个alpha计算一个综合分数。    分数基于三大支柱:    1. 表现力 (40%权重): 基于 Fitness。    2. 效率性 (30%权重): 基于 Margin 和 Returns/Turnover。    3. 风险调整后表现 (30%权重): 基于 收益/回撤 比。    """    df_scores = df.copy()    # --- 步骤1: 计算衍生指标 ---    df_scores['returns_over_turnover'] = np.where(df_scores['turnover'] > 0,                                                  df_scores['returns'] / df_scores['turnover'], 0)       # 【核心改进】计算收益回撤比    # drawdown为0时，给一个极大值，代表风险极小    df_scores['return_to_drawdown'] = np.where(df_scores['drawdown'] > 0,                                               df_scores['returns'] / df_scores['drawdown'],                                               1e6) # 使用一个很大的数    # --- 步骤2: 指标归一化 (转换为0-100分) ---    metrics_to_normalize = {        'fitness': 'higher_is_better',        'returns_over_turnover': 'higher_is_better',        'margin': 'higher_is_better',        'return_to_drawdown': 'higher_is_better' # 【核心改进】新指标也是越高越好    }    for metric, methodology in metrics_to_normalize.items():        min_val = df_scores[metric].min()        max_val = df_scores[metric].max()        if max_val == min_val:            df_scores[f'{metric}_norm'] = 50.0            continue        if methodology == 'higher_is_better':            df_scores[f'{metric}_norm'] = 100 * (df_scores[metric] - min_val) / (max_val - min_val)        # 不再需要 lower_is_better 的 drawdown    # --- 步骤3: 计算三大支柱得分 ---    df_scores['Score_Perf'] = df_scores['fitness_norm']    df_scores['Score_Eff'] = 0.5 * df_scores['returns_over_turnover_norm'] + 0.5 * df_scores['margin_norm']       # 【核心改进】风控力支柱现在变成了风险调整后表现    df_scores['Score_Risk_Adjusted'] = df_scores['return_to_drawdown_norm']    # --- 步骤4: 计算最终综合分数 ---    weights = {        'performance': 0.40,        'efficiency': 0.30,        'risk_adjusted': 0.30 # 权重名称可以相应修改    }    df_scores['Comprehensive_Score'] = (weights['performance'] * df_scores['Score_Perf'] +                                        weights['efficiency'] * df_scores['Score_Eff'] +                                        weights['risk_adjusted'] * df_scores['Score_Risk_Adjusted'])    # --- 步骤5: 准备最终输出 ---    result_df = df_scores[['id', 'Comprehensive_Score', "neutralization"]].copy()    result_df = result_df.sort_values(by='Comprehensive_Score', ascending=False).reset_index(drop=True)    return result_df
```

然后打分，看看结果

```
final_scores_df = calculate_comprehensive_score(df) # df 应为您通过初筛后的alpha列表print(final_scores_df)
```

最后进入第三点：筛选最终进入池子的ppa。

函数如下：

```
def build_portfolio_by_class(    scored_df: pd.DataFrame,    correlation_threshold: float = 0.35,    years_for_corr: int = 4) -> list:    """    通过基于聚类的“轮流选秀”策略构建Alpha组合。    Args:        scored_df (pd.DataFrame): 包含'id', 'Comprehensive_Score', 'neutralization'的DataFrame。        correlation_threshold (float): 相关性的上限阈值。        years_for_corr (int): 用于计算相关性的最近年数。    Returns:        list: 最终入选的alpha ID列表。    """    if scored_df.empty:        print("输入列表为空，无法构建组合。")        return []    # --- 步骤1: 分组和排序 ---    # 1a. 按neutralization分组，并在每个组内按分数降序排序    groups = {        name: group_df.sort_values(by='Comprehensive_Score', ascending=False).reset_index(drop=True)        for name, group_df in scored_df.groupby('neutralization')    }       # 1b. 决定组的遍历顺序：把包含总分第一alpha的组放在最前面    if not scored_df.empty:        top_alpha_group_name = scored_df.iloc[0]['neutralization']        other_group_names = [name for name in groups.keys() if name != top_alpha_group_name]        ordered_group_names = [top_alpha_group_name] + other_group_names    else:        ordered_group_names = list(groups.keys())    print("构建顺序（按组）:", ordered_group_names)    # --- 步骤2: 初始化“选秀”所需变量 ---    selected_alpha_ids = []    selected_pnl_dfs = []    # 为每个组创建一个指针，记录下一轮要从哪个位置开始选    next_candidate_idx = {group_name: 0 for group_name in ordered_group_names}       # --- 步骤3: 开始轮流选秀 ---    round_num = 1    while True:        added_in_this_round = False        print(f"\n=============== 选秀第 {round_num} 轮开始 ===============")        for group_name in ordered_group_names:            print(f"\n--- 轮到组: {group_name} ---")            current_group_df = groups[group_name]                       # 从该组的上一个选中位置开始，寻找下一个合格的候选者            for i in range(next_candidate_idx[group_name], len(current_group_df)):                candidate_row = current_group_df.iloc[i]                candidate_id = candidate_row['id']                               # 如果该alpha因为某种原因已经被选过了，就跳过                if candidate_id in selected_alpha_ids:                    continue                # 【核心逻辑】检查与现有组合的相关性                # 如果是组合的第一个alpha，直接无条件入选                if not selected_alpha_ids:                    max_correlation = 0.0                else:                    # 准备数据进行相关性计算                    os_alpha_pnls = pd.concat(selected_pnl_dfs, axis=1)                    os_alpha_rets = os_alpha_pnls - os_alpha_pnls.ffill().shift(1)                    cutoff_date = pd.to_datetime(os_alpha_rets.index).max() - pd.DateOffset(years=years_for_corr)                    os_alpha_rets = os_alpha_rets[pd.to_datetime(os_alpha_rets.index) > cutoff_date]                                       candidate_pnl_df = _get_alpha_pnl(s, candidate_id).set_index('Date')                    candidate_rets = candidate_pnl_df - candidate_pnl_df.ffill().shift(1)                    candidate_rets = candidate_rets[pd.to_datetime(candidate_rets.index) > cutoff_date]                                       max_correlation = os_alpha_rets.corrwith(candidate_rets.iloc[:, 0]).abs().max()                print(f"  正在评估: {candidate_id} (组内排名 {i+1}), 最大相关性: {max_correlation:.4f}")                # 如果满足条件                if max_correlation < correlation_threshold:                    print(f"  ✅ 结果: 通过! {candidate_id} 已加入组合。")                    selected_alpha_ids.append(candidate_id)                    # 如果是第一个alpha，它的pnl还没有被获取                    if 'candidate_pnl_df' not in locals() or selected_alpha_ids[0] == candidate_id:                        candidate_pnl_df = _get_alpha_pnl(s, candidate_id).set_index('Date')                    selected_pnl_dfs.append(candidate_pnl_df)                                       # 标记本轮有新成员加入                    added_in_this_round = True                    # 更新该组的指针，下一轮从下一个位置开始                    next_candidate_idx[group_name] = i + 1                    # 每个组在本轮只选一个，找到后就跳出，轮到下一个组                    break                else:                    print(f"  ❌ 结果: 拒绝! 相关性超过阈值 {correlation_threshold}。")                       # 如果循环走完了还没找到合适的，说明这个组在本轮选不出人了            else:                print(f"  本轮该组无符合条件的alpha。")               # 如果一整轮下来没有任何新alpha加入，说明选秀结束        if not added_in_this_round:            print("\n=============== 选秀结束 ===============")            print("所有组在本轮都无法提供新的低相关性alpha。")            break               round_num += 1    return selected_alpha_ids
```

然后执行代码，获取最终的结果：

```
print("="*50)print("🚀 开始使用“基于聚类的选秀策略”构建最终Alpha组合...")print("="*50)# 假设 final_scores_df 是您打分后的DataFramefinal_portfolio = build_portfolio_by_class(final_scores_df, correlation_threshold=0.5)print("\n\n" + "="*50)print("🎉 构建完成！最终组合为:")print(final_portfolio)print(f"组合总数: {len(final_portfolio)}")print("="*50)
```

### 帖子 #28: 【代码优化】提供一种【排除厂或者缺失多年数据alpha】的方法，希望有所帮助代码优化
- **主帖链接**: 【代码优化】提供一种【排除厂或者缺失多年数据alpha】的方法希望有所帮助代码优化.md
- **讨论数**: 5

问题背景：在check的时候由于只设置了相关性低的条件，同时因为【厂或者缺失多年数据】的alpha本身就与其他alpha的相关性低，所以经常check出来的alpha点进去一看是厂或者缺失数据的，又需要再一次人工去筛选，加大了人工的时间。解决思路：通过观察注意到，厂或者缺失多年数据的alpha拥有共同特点，就是有很多年份的sharpe值都为0，比如：那么解决的方式就是，获取到上述表格每年的shapre，然后通过判断等于0的年份有几年即可。常听到说最好交8年有数据的alpha，那么判断条件就是sharpe不等于0的年份大于8就可以了。最终代码：def check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):# Get the yearly stats dataa = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()data = a['records']# Extract sharpe values (7th parameter in each record, index 6)sharpe_values = [float(record[6]) for record in data]# Check conditions:# 1. At least 8 years with sharpe != 0non_zero_sharpe = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe != 0)condition1 = non_zero_sharpe >= 8# Return True if both conditions are metreturn condition1上面代码先获取每年的sharpe数据，然后保存到列表中，最后判断sharpe不为0的年份是否大于8即可。代码扩展：除了拥有8年数据外，一般还可以要求至少6年的shapre大于1，从而保证alpha的稳健性。也可以要求2022年shapre大于1，从而保证近几年的情况良好，不至于说sharpe高是只是因为旧年份导致的。代码改进：def check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):# Get the yearly stats dataa = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()data = a['records']# Extract sharpe values (7th parameter in each record, index 6)sharpe_values = [float(record[6]) for record in data]# Check conditions:# 1. At least 8 years with sharpe != 0non_zero_sharpe = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe != 0)condition1 = non_zero_sharpe >= 8# 2. At least 6 years with sharpe > 1sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe > 1)condition2 = sharpe_above_1 >= 6print(alpha_id+":sharpe检测:"+str(condition1 and condition2 and  data[9][6]>0.8))# Return True if both conditions are metreturn condition1 and condition2 and  data[9][6]>1  #2022年的sharpe大于1第一个条件依然是8年shapre不为0，第二个条件是至少有6年的shapre大于1。最终的data[9][6]>1的意思是2022年的sharpe大于1。2013-2023年中2022年的是第10年，索引是9，sharpe数据在api的['records']的索引是6，所以是data[9][6]。你也可以扩展自己的条件。补充：获取api的方式可以按【f12-网络-然后刷新网页-名称列表-标头】进行查询。比如上述代码中的api来源如下：然后通过【响应】来看获取到的数据结构是如何的：代码补充：代码中用到了wait_get方法，是其他顾问提供的，用session基本的get方法也可以有同样的效果，该方法是进行了一些改进，增加了等待时间的get。def wait_get(s,url: str, max_retries: int = 10) -> "Response":"""发送带有重试机制的 GET 请求，直到成功或达到最大重试次数。此函数会根据服务器返回的 `Retry-After` 头信息进行等待，并在遇到 401 状态码时重新初始化配置。Args:url (str): 目标 URL。max_retries (int, optional): 最大重试次数，默认为 10。Returns:Response: 请求的响应对象。"""retries = 0while retries < max_retries:while True:simulation_progress = s.get(url)if simulation_progress.headers.get("Retry-After", 0) == 0:breaktime.sleep(float(simulation_progress.headers["Retry-After"]))if simulation_progress.status_code < 400:breakelse:time.sleep(2 ** retries)retries += 1return simulation_progress希望对大家有所帮助，一起进步！！

### 帖子 #29: 【代码优化】提供一种【排除厂或者缺失多年数据alpha】的方法，希望有所帮助代码优化
- **主帖链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com【代码优化】提供一种【排除厂或者缺失多年数据alpha】的方法希望有所帮助代码优化_33369193826199.md
- **讨论数**: 5

**问题背景** ：在check的时候由于只设置了相关性低的条件，同时因为【厂或者缺失多年数据】的alpha本身就与其他alpha的相关性低，所以经常check出来的alpha点进去一看是厂或者缺失数据的，又需要再一次人工去筛选，加大了人工的时间。

**解决思路** ：通过观察注意到，厂或者缺失多年数据的alpha拥有共同特点，就是有很多年份的sharpe值都为0，比如：

那么解决的方式就是，获取到上述表格每年的shapre，然后通过判断等于0的年份有几年即可。常听到说最好交8年有数据的alpha，那么判断条件就是sharpe不等于0的年份大于8就可以了。

**最终代码** ：

```
def check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):    # Get the yearly stats data    a = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()    data = a['records']       # Extract sharpe values (7th parameter in each record, index 6)    sharpe_values = [float(record[6]) for record in data]       # Check conditions:    # 1. At least 8 years with sharpe != 0    non_zero_sharpe = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe != 0)    condition1 = non_zero_sharpe >= 8       # Return True if both conditions are met    return condition1 
```

上面代码先获取每年的sharpe数据，然后保存到列表中，最后判断sharpe不为0的年份是否大于8即可。

**代码扩展** ：除了拥有8年数据外，一般还可以要求至少6年的shapre大于1，从而保证alpha的稳健性。也可以要求2022年shapre大于1，从而保证近几年的情况良好，不至于说sharpe高是只是因为旧年份导致的。

**代码改进** ：

```
def check_alpha_sharpe_conditions(s, alpha_id):    # Get the yearly stats data    a = wait_get(s, f"[链接已屏蔽]).json()    data = a['records']       # Extract sharpe values (7th parameter in each record, index 6)    sharpe_values = [float(record[6]) for record in data]       # Check conditions:    # 1. At least 8 years with sharpe != 0    non_zero_sharpe = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe != 0)    condition1 = non_zero_sharpe >= 8       # 2. At least 6 years with sharpe > 1    sharpe_above_1 = sum(1 for sharpe in sharpe_values if sharpe > 1)    condition2 = sharpe_above_1 >= 6    print(alpha_id+":sharpe检测:"+str(condition1 and condition2 and  data[9][6]>0.8))       # Return True if both conditions are met    return condition1 and condition2 and  data[9][6]>1  #2022年的sharpe大于1
```

第一个条件依然是8年shapre不为0，第二个条件是至少有6年的shapre大于1。最终的data[9][6]>1的意思是2022年的sharpe大于1。2013-2023年中2022年的是第10年，索引是9，sharpe数据在api的['records']的索引是6，所以是data[9][6]。你也可以扩展自己的条件。

**补充** ：获取api的方式可以按【f12-网络-然后刷新网页-名称列表-标头】进行查询。

比如上述代码中的api来源如下：

**代码补充** ：

代码中用到了wait_get方法，是其他顾问提供的，用session基本的get方法也可以有同样的效果，该方法是进行了一些改进，增加了等待时间的get。

```
def wait_get(s,url: str, max_retries: int = 10) -> "Response":    """    发送带有重试机制的 GET 请求，直到成功或达到最大重试次数。    此函数会根据服务器返回的 `Retry-After` 头信息进行等待，并在遇到 401 状态码时重新初始化配置。    Args:        url (str): 目标 URL。        max_retries (int, optional): 最大重试次数，默认为 10。    Returns:        Response: 请求的响应对象。    """    retries = 0    while retries < max_retries:        while True:            simulation_progress = s.get(url)            if simulation_progress.headers.get("Retry-After", 0) == 0:                break            time.sleep(float(simulation_progress.headers["Retry-After"]))        if simulation_progress.status_code < 400:            break        else:            time.sleep(2 ** retries)            retries += 1    return simulation_progress
```

希望对大家有所帮助，一起进步！！

### 探讨 #3: 关于《PnL = ∑(Robustness * Creativity)》的评论回复

### 探讨 #11: 关于《ALLOCATION OF OSMOSIS POINTS GUIDE.》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] ALLOCATION OF OSMOSIS POINTS GUIDE.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Thanks for the clear breakdown. One additional nuance: while uniform allocation is simpler, diversifying points based on expected performance (e.g., higher to alphas with stronger backtest consistency) can improve overall Osmosis resilience. Also, remember that each region and delay is independent—so you can treat them as separate portfolios. Don’t forget to monitor correlation among your chosen alphas; putting too many points on highly correlated signals reduces the benefit of having 10+ alphas.

---

### 探讨 #14: 关于《alpha ideas》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] alpha ideas.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Higher decay  smooths the alpha, reduces turnover, and often improves fitness if the signal is noisy—but it can flatten the ladder shape by lowering responsiveness. Lower decay  keeps the alpha more reactive, increasing turnover and potentially sharpening the ladder, but may hurt stability. There's no universal "recommended" value; try starting around 5 and optimize based on your alpha's half-life and backtest results.

---

### 探讨 #15: 关于《alpha ideas》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] alpha ideas_39212369291031.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Higher decay  smooths the alpha, reduces turnover, and often improves fitness if the signal is noisy—but it can flatten the ladder shape by lowering responsiveness. Lower decay  keeps the alpha more reactive, increasing turnover and potentially sharpening the ladder, but may hurt stability. There's no universal "recommended" value; try starting around 5 and optimize based on your alpha's half-life and backtest results.

Great practical advice, especially the emphasis on robustness across different market regimes rather than just backtest fit. One thing I’d add: always stress-test alphas with out-of-sample data and simple sensitivity checks (e.g., small parameter shifts or removing extreme days). That extra layer of validation often separates a lucky idea from a genuinely repeatable signal. Thanks for sharing this.

### 探讨 #34: 关于《Exploring Implied Volatility Spread as an Alpha Signal》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] Exploring Implied Volatility Spread as an Alpha Signal_40213475309719.md
- **评论时间**: 1个月前

Interesting idea — using the call-put IV spread as a sentiment signal makes intuitive sense. To improve robustness across regimes, you could try applying a longer-term  `ts_zscore`  or  `ts_rank`  relative to each stock’s own history, rather than just cross-sectional rank. Also testing different lookbacks for the spread calculation might help reduce noise.

### 探讨 #35: 关于《Financial Signal Indicators and Trading Rules》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Financial Signal Indicators and Trading Rules.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Nice breakdown — combining multiple signal types definitely helps reduce reliance on any single noisy indicator. One thing I’d add: when mixing signals like earnings growth, volatility spreads, and sentiment, it’s crucial to check their correlation and stability across regimes. Otherwise, the ensemble might look robust in‑sample but fall apart when market conditions shift. Have you experimented with time‑varying weights instead of fixed rules?

### 探讨 #41: 关于《group_cartesian_product(g1, g2) 運算子介紹》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] group_cartesian_productg1 g2 運算子介紹.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

很清晰的笛卡儿积用法解释。补充一点实践中容易踩的坑：当 g1 和 g2 各自有较多类别时，组合数 n×m 会快速膨胀。比如行业 10 个 × 市值分位 10 个 = 100 组，若全市场只有 2000 只股票，平均每组 20 只，勉强可用；但如果再用第三层分位数就会过细。建议先用  `group_count`  检查每个子群的大小，低于 10~15 只时  `group_neutralize`  可能很不稳定。另外，该算子也适合构建“双重分组”下的排序策略，比如先按行业×市值分箱，再在箱内做  `rank` ，能有效消除行业和规模的共同影响。

---

### 探讨 #42: 关于《group_cartesian_product(g1, g2) 運算子介紹》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] group_cartesian_productg1 g2 運算子介紹_39210414994967.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

很清晰的笛卡儿积用法解释。补充一点实践中容易踩的坑：当 g1 和 g2 各自有较多类别时，组合数 n×m 会快速膨胀。比如行业 10 个 × 市值分位 10 个 = 100 组，若全市场只有 2000 只股票，平均每组 20 只，勉强可用；但如果再用第三层分位数就会过细。建议先用  `group_count`  检查每个子群的大小，低于 10~15 只时  `group_neutralize`  可能很不稳定。另外，该算子也适合构建“双重分组”下的排序策略，比如先按行业×市值分箱，再在箱内做  `rank` ，能有效消除行业和规模的共同影响。

---

### 探讨 #43: 关于《Handling Sparse Alternative Datasets: Event-Driven Thinking?》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Handling Sparse Alternative Datasets Event-Driven Thinking.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

**Great discussion,** framing sparse data as event-driven is a smart shift. Building on KP26017’s decay idea — you could also use  **time-decayed ranks**  (e.g.,  `ts_rank`  on time-since-event with exponential decay) to preserve ordinal information while naturally handling gaps. Another angle: combine event indicators with a low-latency continuous feature (e.g., volume or volatility spikes) using  `group_neutralize`  or conditional operators — this can amplify the event signal without overfitting to empty days. Would love to hear if anyone has tried blending sparse filings with real-time pricing residuals.

---

### 探讨 #44: 关于《Handling Sparse Alternative Datasets: Event-Driven Thinking?》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] Handling Sparse Alternative Datasets Event-Driven Thinking_39650029114903.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

**Great discussion,** framing sparse data as event-driven is a smart shift. Building on KP26017’s decay idea — you could also use  **time-decayed ranks**  (e.g.,  `ts_rank`  on time-since-event with exponential decay) to preserve ordinal information while naturally handling gaps. Another angle: combine event indicators with a low-latency continuous feature (e.g., volume or volatility spikes) using  `group_neutralize`  or conditional operators — this can amplify the event signal without overfitting to empty days. Would love to hear if anyone has tried blending sparse filings with real-time pricing residuals.

---

### 探讨 #45: 关于《High Turnover Alphas: Think in Terms of Information, Not Turnover》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] High Turnover Alphas Think in Terms of Information Not Turnover.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Great discussion. I completely agree that high turnover should follow from information decay, not be forced for its own sake. One nuance worth adding: when turnover emerges naturally from fast‑decaying signals, we still need to explicitly model transaction costs and market impact. A signal that turns over every few hours may be profitable in theory, but if the edge per trade is too small to cover slippage, the alpha becomes unactionable. So beyond quantifying information decay, I think we should also estimate the break‑even turnover for each signal—where the marginal cost equals the marginal expected return. This helps separate genuinely useful high‑turnover alphas from those that are just “noisy but fast.” Thanks for sparking this discussion.

---

- **评论时间**: 2个月前

### 探讨 #49: 关于《How to balance signal strength and turnover in alpha design?》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] How to balance signal strength and turnover in alpha design.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Great discussion, Lucy – and PD97561, your point about smoothing operators is spot on.

Another technique I've found helpful is applying  **truncation**  (e.g.,  `truncate` ) before ranking, especially when using z-score or winsorization. Extreme values often cause positions to flip violently from period to period. By capping them, turnover can drop noticeably without a big hit to signal strength.

Also, combining a  **slow trend**  (e.g., 10‑day decay) with a  **fast confirmation**  (e.g., 2‑day change) – then using  `ts_rank`  on the composite – sometimes keeps fitness high while reducing unnecessary churn.

Curious if others have tried using  `ts_sum`  over a short window as a lightweight smoother instead of full exponential decay.

Thanks for bringing up this trade‑off – it’s really at the heart of robust alpha design.

---

- **评论时间**: 2个月前

### 探讨 #55: 关于《Improvement of an alpha using the decay operator on an Analyst Net Income Signal.》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Improvement of an alpha using the decay operator on an Analyst Net Income Signal.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Nice and clean use of linear decay on analyst net income revisions. A couple of suggestions to take it further: (1) test other decay shapes like exponential or hyperbolic to see if they better capture the fading impact of earnings surprises, and (2) consider neutralizing the signal against sector or market factors — analyst expectation changes often have strong common components. Also, have you checked the turnover and whether the decay window of 5 is robust across different market regimes? Thanks for sharing the idea.

---

### 探讨 #59: 关于《IQC IS Score Increasing》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] IQC IS Score Increasing.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

From my experience, high-impact alphas often come from combining unconventional data fields or applying non‑linear transformations that reveal a genuinely new market edge, not just tweaking common factors. Uniqueness matters just as much as Sharpe and fitness because the scoring system rewards diversification; even a lower‑performing alpha can boost your IQC IS score significantly if it’s uncorrelated with your existing alphas. Instead of chasing many small improvements, I focus on a few deeply different ideas—e.g., using alternative deflators or cross‑sectional ranks—which tend to add 500+ points each when they pass. Try analyzing the correlation matrix of your current alphas, then deliberately build something that moves in the opposite direction of your highest‑weighted ones.

---

Try analyzing the correlation matrix of your current alphas, then deliberately build something that moves in the opposite direction of your highest‑weighted ones.

### 探讨 #63: 关于《Neutralization Strategy》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Neutralization Strategy.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

The choice depends on where your alpha lives: neutralize only the factors that add noise, not the ones that drive returns. Partial neutralization (e.g., sector but not market) often improves performance when the signal has legitimate exposure to a broad group. Test both—full neutralization isn’t always optimal.

---

### 探讨 #73: 关于《Strategies for improving Fitness without sacrificing Sharpe Ratio》的评论回复

Thanks for sharing this — balancing Fitness and Sharpe is a real challenge. In my experience, adding a mild  `ts_rank`  or  `ts_zscore`  after neutralization helps reduce correlation without destroying the signal. Also, slightly increasing the decay on your price‑volume terms can lower turnover while keeping Sharpe surprisingly stable. Have you tried testing different neutralization windows (e.g., 20 vs 60 days) for your sector adjustments?

### 探讨 #75: 关于《tail(x, lower, upper, newval) 運算子介紹》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] tailx lower upper newval 運算子介紹.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

很实用的介绍，尤其喜欢信号修剪和极值分组的案例。补充一点： `tail`  是 **开区间** 判定，如果想把边界值也纳入替换，可以配合  `x <= lower`  或  `x >= upper`  做预处理，或者直接用  `ifelse` 。另外， `tail`  和  `replace`  配合  `ts_rank`  等时序算子一起使用时，注意  `newval`  必须是常数，不能是动态值，这点容易踩坑。

---

很实用的介绍，尤其喜欢信号修剪和极值分组的案例。补充一点： `tail`  是 **开区间** 判定，如果想把边界值也纳入替换，可以配合  `x <= lower`  或  `x >= upper`  做预处理，或者直接用  `ifelse` 。另外， `tail`  和  `replace`  配合  `ts_rank`  等时序算子一起使用时，注意  `newval`  必须是常数，不能是动态值，这点容易踩坑。

### 探讨 #77: 关于《Trade_when vs Daily rebalancing》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Trade_when vs Daily rebalancing.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

`trade_when`  tends to outperform when your alpha is state‑dependent—e.g., momentum only works during high volume. The condition filters out low‑signal periods, while the longer hold reduces turnover, both boosting Sharpe. Adjusting decay just changes how fast a position fades;  `trade_when`  controls  *if*  you trade at all. So use  `trade_when`  when the signal’s strength depends on a regime, and stick with decay when the signal itself is continuous but mean‑reverting.

---

### 探讨 #78: 关于《Trade_when vs Daily rebalancing》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] Trade_when vs Daily rebalancing_39374110020503.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

`trade_when`  tends to outperform when your alpha is state‑dependent—e.g., momentum only works during high volume. The condition filters out low‑signal periods, while the longer hold reduces turnover, both boosting Sharpe. Adjusting decay just changes how fast a position fades;  `trade_when`  controls  *if*  you trade at all. So use  `trade_when`  when the signal’s strength depends on a regime, and stick with decay when the signal itself is continuous but mean‑reverting.

### 探讨 #79: 关于《Understanding Sentiment Data in Simple Terms》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Understanding Sentiment Data in Simple Terms.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Great explanation for beginners. One nuance worth adding: sentiment data works best when combined with volume and volatility signals. For example, extremely high positive sentiment on low volume often fades quickly, while moderate positive sentiment with rising volume can signal sustained momentum. Also, be mindful of sentiment divergence—when price moves up but sentiment turns neutral or negative, it's often a leading indicator of reversal. Thanks for starting this useful thread.

---

### 探讨 #81: 关于《Understanding Time-Series Ranking in Alpha Evaluation》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] Understanding Time-Series Ranking in Alpha Evaluation_39526836152599.md
- **评论时间**: 1个月前

Great discussion.  `ts_rank`  is indeed powerful for normalizing signals across time, but as noted, it can also amplify noise when the lookback window is too short or the underlying data is non‑stationary. I've found it works best when combined with a smoothing operator like  `ts_mean`  before ranking. Also worth testing different window lengths to avoid over‑reacting to recent outliers.

### 探讨 #85: 关于《Weight Concentration Control》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] Weight Concentration Control_39760160578839.md
- **评论时间**: 1个月前

Great tip! I'd also add that applying a  **capping/flooring**  step after z-score (e.g., winsorizing at 3 or 4 sigma) can further reduce the impact of extreme weights. Combining  `ts_backfill`  with  `group_backfill`  can also help when the missing patterns differ across assets. Have you experimented with decay factors in the backfill window to give more weight to recent observations? Thanks for sharing!

---

### 探讨 #86: 关于《What Comes First — The Idea or the Data?》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] What Comes First  The Idea or the Data.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

I usually start with a basic hypothesis based on market intuition or observation, then test it quickly with data. That said, exploratory data analysis is equally valuable — the two approaches work best in tandem. A weak initial idea might reveal something unexpected when you look at the data first, and vice versa. Iterating between hypothesis and exploration often leads to more robust alphas.

---

### 探讨 #90: 关于《Why did the GLB region have four years of data with zero entries?》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] Why did the GLB region have four years of data with zero entries.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Yes, this is completely normal. This GLB dataset does not contain any entries for the 2014–2017 period, likely because the data coverage starts after 2017. In other words, those years fall outside the dataset's available time range — effectively, the dataset didn't exist or wasn't populated back then.

---

### 探讨 #91: 关于《Why did the GLB region have four years of data with zero entries?》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] Why did the GLB region have four years of data with zero entries_39704263249303.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

Yes, this is completely normal. This GLB dataset does not contain any entries for the 2014–2017 period, likely because the data coverage starts after 2017. In other words, those years fall outside the dataset's available time range — effectively, the dataset didn't exist or wasn't populated back then.

### 探讨 #107: 关于《PnL = ∑(Robustness * Creativity)》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] 【VF 095收入经验分享】高VF如何拿到更高的base经验分享.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

感谢你的分享。下面我介绍一下社区分的构成。

1.会议

参加会议30分钟以上可以加分

2.拉人

让别人注册的时候用你的推荐码。不过这个需要一定的宣传能力

3.评论+发帖

成功评论+发帖后不是马上加分的。需要点赞。

Likes in the current quarter on a comment published in current quarter (min. length 100 chars)

10 to 19 likes: 0.1

20 to 49 likes: 0.2

>50 likes: 0.5

Likes in the current quarter on a post published in current quarter (min. length 100 chars)

10 to 19 likes: 1

20 to 49 likes: 2

>50 likes: 5

可以看到点赞数 **至少要大于10才有分加** ！，比如贴主这个帖子，目前帖子是6点赞，发出来帖子其实很好，但是没有超过10，对社区分来说相当于没有帮助。所以还需要想办法让其他的热心顾问来给你点赞才可以的。

祝好！（我给你点赞啦，所以目前是7个点赞啦~~~）

---

### 探讨 #132: 关于《快速了解operator：group_zscore》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] 快速了解operatorgroup_zscore.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

感谢您对  `group_zscore`  的清晰讲解！分組標準化在處理行業、市值或板塊等類別資料時確實非常實用，能有效消除組間基線差異，讓信號更純淨。補充一點實務考量：使用時請留意分組內的樣本數量——若某組樣本過少（例如少於 5-10 檔標的），計算出的平均值和標準差可能不穩定，導致標準化後的訊號帶有較大雜訊。另外，可以嘗試將  `group_zscore`  與時間序列運算符（如  `ts_rank` ）串聯使用，先捕捉個股自身的相對強弱，再在組內比較，效果往往更好。期待您繼續推出 operator 系列，很有幫助！

---

- **评论时间**: 2个月前

### 探讨 #134: 关于《快速了解operator：ts_returns》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] 快速了解operatorts_returns.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

感谢您对  `ts_returns`  运算符的详细解读！文章结构清晰，从定义、用途到两种模式的计算公式都讲得很明白，对初学者很有帮助。补充一点小建议：实际使用时， `mode=2` （对称回报率）除了能减小极端值影响，还能避免分母为零的情况（当  `ts_delay(x,d)`  接近0时）。另外，滚动窗口  `d`  的选择可以结合标的的波动率或交易频率来调整。期待您分享更多 operator 的实战心得！

---

### 探讨 #136: 关于《快速了解operator：ts_scale》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] 快速了解operatorts_scale.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

感谢分享！对  `ts_scale`  的解读很实用，尤其是指出它相比  `scale`  或  `rank`  更能保留信号强度，这点对 Alpha 优化非常关键。补充一点：公式中的  `constant`  参数除了默认的 0，有时可以设为 1 或其他值来调整输出范围（例如映射到 [1,2] 区间），方便后续组合。另外， `ts_scale`  对异常值敏感，如果数据有极端噪声，可以先做 winsorize 处理。期待您继续推出更多 operator 系列内容！

---

### 探讨 #142: 关于《新手课代码分享》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] 新手课代码分享.md
- **评论时间**: 1个月前

这篇代码分享很实用，尤其是批量生成alpha的思路值得学习。不过直接运行确实容易遇到语法错误，比如 `group_mean` 需要三个参数，而嵌套循环里只传了两个；另外 `data_type='GROUP'` 得到的字段大多不适用于 `ts_mean` 这类时序操作，建议改为 `MATRIX` 并检查API参数。期待后续能加上简单的表达式校验和结果过滤机制，减少无效提交。对新手来说，理解平台API的字段类型和算子约束比单纯跑通代码更重要。

---

### 探讨 #143: 关于《新手课代码分享》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] 新手课代码分享_39467969845783.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

这篇代码分享很实用，尤其是批量生成alpha的思路值得学习。不过直接运行确实容易遇到语法错误，比如 `group_mean` 需要三个参数，而嵌套循环里只传了两个；另外 `data_type='GROUP'` 得到的字段大多不适用于 `ts_mean` 这类时序操作，建议改为 `MATRIX` 并检查API参数。期待后续能加上简单的表达式校验和结果过滤机制，减少无效提交。对新手来说，理解平台API的字段类型和算子约束比单纯跑通代码更重要。

---

### 探讨 #144: 关于《研发alpha注意点》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: [Commented] 研发alpha注意点.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

这篇关于WorldQuant BRAIN平台开发Alpha的注意事项非常实用，尤其适合刚入门或者希望提升因子通过率的研究顾问。文章抓住了几个关键痛点：一是强调“经济逻辑”而非盲目堆砌算子，很多新人容易陷入过度拟合的陷阱；二是低相关性策略，结合行业中性化确实是突破拥挤赛道的有效手段；三是对换手率、回撤等稳定性指标的量化建议非常具体，可操作性强。

我自己在开发过程中也深有体会：单纯追求高夏普很容易忽略因子的可解释性，而人工审核环节往往更看重逻辑是否自洽。另外，文中提到的“从金融学术论文中找灵感”是一条被验证过的捷径，建议开发者多关注那些在A股或新兴市场尚未被广泛应用的异象因子。

唯一想补充的是，对于兼职开发者而言，算力资源和数据范围有限，初期不妨先从基本面或分析师数据中的简单信号入手，再逐步引入复杂的时序算子，这样迭代效率会更高。期待作者后续能分享一些关于组合优化或因子衰减的实际案例。

---

### 探讨 #145: 关于《研发alpha注意点》的评论回复
- **帖子链接**: https://support.worldquantbrain.com[Commented] 研发alpha注意点_39592467967639.md
- **评论时间**: 2个月前

这篇关于WorldQuant BRAIN平台开发Alpha的注意事项非常实用，尤其适合刚入门或者希望提升因子通过率的研究顾问。文章抓住了几个关键痛点：一是强调“经济逻辑”而非盲目堆砌算子，很多新人容易陷入过度拟合的陷阱；二是低相关性策略，结合行业中性化确实是突破拥挤赛道的有效手段；三是对换手率、回撤等稳定性指标的量化建议非常具体，可操作性强。
